## <a name="windows-server-2012"></a><span data-ttu-id="dc778-1991">Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc778-1991">Windows Server 2012</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="dc778-1992">Atributos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dc778-1992">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2012-attributes)
